The Annual Cultural festival of IEM - IEMPACT '18 has returned, bigger and better.
In accordance to the announcement, to showcase the inner eye we have incorporated the event "Short Film making Contest". In light of the fact that the event requires elaborate preparations, we are announcing the RULES here early.
• Film makers are encouraged to send their work, with a running time of "8+2 minutes".
• Entry fee is Rs. 500/- per individual/group.
• Participants are requested to send their Short Film along with a short write up on the film and a brief biography of the film maker, in not more than 100 words at: iempact18@gmail.com.
• Film should be in English / Hindi/ Bengali. Non-English films should have English subtitles.
• Deadline for film submission: January 18th, 2018. Deadline for fees submission: January 4th - January 18th (excluding Mondays, Sundays and prominent holidays) at IEM Gurukul Campus (Address mentioned at the end).
• The Top 3 selected entries will be screened at the 2nd day of the festival (Dates to be announced soon).
• All of the films, whose entry had been submitted would be given a ‘Certificate of Participation’. The top three would receive winner certificates on the day of the screening.
• The top three films will receive cash prizes.
• All Submissions must be made in : .mp4 format.
• Entries can be as individual or group submission representing a college or an institution.
• Submissions are limited to ONE entry per group/individual.
• In appropriate and objectionable content will not be accepted. Failure to abide by this will result in the immediate disqualification of the entry
• Submissions must be restricted to 2D media.
• Any rule is subject to change if deemed necessary by the authorities. For further details:
